  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_78ca57e7-c45a-459f-b9ab-edda883c0cda'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

<a href="/questions/579477-ok-so-i-have-ordered-the-fallen-series-but">Ok so I have ordered the Fallen series but I missed out Fallen in Love, do I need to read this one before I read the 5th book? I see there is a lot of bad reviews about this series but I loved the hush hush saga so I am hoping these are just as good!</a>
</div>

<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">No, technically, you do not need to read any of the Fallen books in order to read the book Unforgiven cause this story is about Cam and not Daniel and<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">No, technically, you do not need to read any of the Fallen books in order to read the book Unforgiven cause this story is about Cam and not Daniel and Luce. Fallen in Love is based on Arriane, and so you don't really need to read it. The Fallen series are really good, most of the people judge on the first book which is quite stereotypical but the second, third and fourth book is really good, so if you really want a plot twist and an interesting story line you must keep reading. I hope this helps :)<a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>
</span>
</div>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer216093183" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1637563091699754172"><b> Post-review: </b> I feel like, after reading almost all of this series, now, including the in-between book that I was in no way obligated to read, I am allowed to write a letter. I feel as if we have grown......so much closer over this series. <i> So much closer.....</i>:<br/><br/><i> My dearest Lauren Kate; my honey-bun, my up-and-downer; my peach, </i><br/><br/>I regret to inform you that your writing has gone all-out bipolar on us all, and this book is prime evidence of that fact. Passion was the worst book of this series to dat</span>
  <span id="freeText1637563091699754172" style="display:none"><b> Post-review: </b> I feel like, after reading almost all of this series, now, including the in-between book that I was in no way obligated to read, I am allowed to write a letter. I feel as if we have grown......so much closer over this series. <i> So much closer.....</i>:<br><br><i> My dearest Lauren Kate; my honey-bun, my up-and-downer; my peach, </i><br><br>I regret to inform you that your writing has gone all-out bipolar on us all, and this book is prime evidence of that fact. Passion was the worst book of this series to date before this book was published, in my honest opinion, and I believe that Fallen In Love was <i> your </i> honest attempt at rectifying the train wreck that your last book was. You were trying to follow that old saying:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380360115ra/711012.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i> I think that the lawn mower really makes the scene. Take some notes, Katey-waty. </i><br><br>Sad to say that you tried, and you failed. Your lawn mower never even got off the ground; it kind of wobbled off into the air just a little bit, but when you had your excerpt of Rapture in there it just exploded into a fiery blaze. Seriously. It was so huge it burned my hands. Be expecting the medical bill from the hospital either also inclosed inside this envelope or as a later package a couple of days after.<br><br> Let's go over your first story in this little four-story <s> headache </s> extravaganza. To be blunt with you, dearest, it really was not good. The whole romance with Shelby and Miles was so awkward, not well-written and just......plain old shit. Don't get me wrong, my little cup-Kate, I'm extremely glad that there isn't a love triangle anymore (although you either purposefully or accidentally decided to hint at Luce with Cam again in the Rapture excerpt <s> shoot me now </s>) between them, but it was just bad. Here's some of those awkward first-story gems:<br><br><i>Then I realized it was just me and Miles.<br>Alone. </i><br><br>And another gem at basically the very beginning:<br><br><i> "I thought we were home!" Shelby cried, her voice landing <b> somewhere between a bark and a whine. </b> </i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380360115i/711013.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i> Why, Katie boo-bear? Why? </i><br><br>Did you <i> just </i> realize that, Shelby? After, even in your own words, an "eternity" of jumping through time with mainly just Miles that little light-bulb of thought finally entered your character's dim little brain? Just because you feel the need to write another story and milk out this series does <i> not </i> mean that you can randomly write a relationship between two characters that was never even hinted at before! If you're going to write a love triangle and dig yourself into that terrible, dark, hole then you'd damn well come up with a fantastic way to get out of it! The whole passage was just Shelby having a fetish for Miles' damned hat and a really random make-out sesh at the end. And what the hell? A <i> bark </i> and a <i> whine? </i> What is Shelby, a <s> bitch </s> dog? I tried making that noise myself and it either sounded like I had a speech impediment or, well, a dog. I understand what you were <i> trying </i> to say, but you didn't say it at all correctly, sugar. I feel as if, Katie dear, if you had just left out that story I could have given this book possibly even three stars even <i> with </i> the Rapture-disaster at the end! <br><br>I'm sorry, Katydid. I didn't mean to get mad, because you really did redeem yourself in the middle two series.<br><br>Now, mon petit chou, I want you to guess why I liked the next two stories. Really, just guess. No? Okay, then I'll tell you: <b> BECAUSE IT WASN'T ABOUT LUCE OR DANIEL! </b> <s>I'm sorry, sweetie, I couldn't keep it in. </s> I was actually about the side characters that I could stand, and I honestly think that their stories, if they were elongated, would be better than this whole Fallen series. I'm not even kidding right now. Now, Kate, I am still not in any way saying that the two other stories you wrote (omitting the one about Luce as the last story which was still decent in comparison to some other Luce's.....other visits to her past) were fantastic, but they were <i> still </i> tolerable <i> and </i> readable, <i> and </i> actually had a good kind of message <i> and </i> Arianne and Roland actually <i> learned </i> from what happened to both of them because of love <i> and </i> had decent character development with an again somewhat decent moral/lesson at the end! Those two stories (which I may or may not elaborate on some more when it isn't so late <s> and I know where the damned book is </s>) were just another concrete example as to how what you think is someone being pessimistic and foolish are the people that are actually <i> decent; </i> not the ones whom you think are the ones in "real love"<br><br>I just wish you had written the rest as you did with Roland and Arrianne, Kate. <br><br><i> With dearest regards your amazing, intelligent, beautiful, incredible, and ineffably sagacious, <br><br>Caitlin. </i><br><br>Oh, and as an added aside: I would write about Rapture in this review, but I have so much rage for even those first damned fifteen pages or so that I'm going to write about <i> all </i> of my feelings in a Rapture pre-review in the next couple of days, so be ready for that one, folks.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380360117ra/711014.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>And I just added this gif because I can. Good day to you all. <br><br><b> Pre-review: </b> Bhahahahahahahaha! This quote.....oh this quote..... (this was the synopsis before my dear Goodreads friend-and librarian- changed it to what it is now)<br><br><i> This book is about the only Valentine's day that Luce and Daniel ever had together. How romantic and heartbreaking is that? </i><br><br>*picks up the supposed "book" *<br><br>BHAHAHAAHAHAHAAHAH!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380360117ra/711015.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380360117ra/711016.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/250568.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>How romantic, and *splutters* <i> heartbreaking? </i><br><br>This has got to be one of the best practical jokes I've ever heard of in my life!! Now, come on, someone 'fess up. It was funny while it lasted, but come on now. Somebody own up. Was it you, Cillian?<br><br>*looks around and sees nobody*<br><br>Okay, if not Cillian, than maybe Mocha?<br><br>*still sees nobody and grows panicked* <br><br>Anyone?! Come on; this is just way to corny to be an actual <i> book! </i><br><br>*cricket cricket*<br><br>Wait.....so this isn't a joke?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380360117ra/711017.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Oh my God I am officially horrified. This is actually <i> a book?!?!? </i> <br><br>I am........astounded. Is Lauren Kate seriously this <s> greedy </s> desperate for money that she writes about Luce and Daniel.....on Valentine's Day, no less? That is seriously the epitome of cliche and horribleness! I can't....I can't......understand.....brain.....fried....<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380345572ra/700204.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="1637563091699754172" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer7399199763147878114"><b>(scroll for review)</b><br/><br/>They REALLY need to stop screwing with Fernanda's art!!!<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380360439i/711361._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><br/><br/><br/><br/><br/><br/><br/><br/><br/><br/><br/><br/>Wow. What a complete waste of paper. <br/><br/>The last time I checked, a "novel" was more than two-hundred measly pages of huge text and lots of chapter breaks. Calling this tiny thing a "novel" is ridiculous, as is pricing it at $15.99. Luckily, I got it on sale at Target, so it wasn't too expensive, but I totally want my money back after reading it.<br/><br/>Also, the last time I checked, a novel in a series was supposed to advance the ov</span>
  <span id="freeText7399199763147878114" style="display:none"><b>(scroll for review)</b><br><br>They REALLY need to stop screwing with Fernanda's art!!!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380360439i/711361._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br>Wow. What a complete waste of paper. <br><br>The last time I checked, a "novel" was more than two-hundred measly pages of huge text and lots of chapter breaks. Calling this tiny thing a "novel" is ridiculous, as is pricing it at $15.99. Luckily, I got it on sale at Target, so it wasn't too expensive, but I totally want my money back after reading it.<br><br>Also, the last time I checked, a novel in a series was supposed to advance the overall plot. At least a little. In FALLEN IN LOVE, the word "plot" is nonexistent. Cute, sappy valentine's day stories aren't enough to satisfy your readers, Kate. The franchise doesn't need to be milked any more. Honestly, I would've rather gotten RAPTURE after a normal nine-month period than wait another three for this piece of crap to be released.<br><br>The first story in FALLEN IN LOVE is the story of Miles and Shelby. This was my favorite (and the only one I actually liked). So much of it was backstory and background and description, and so little of it was actual character development, plot, you know, stuff a book needs to thrive? Even though I liked the romance between Shelby and Miles, I wasn't completely enthralled about everything else.<br><br>The second story in the book is the story of Roland. I also liked his story, but I wouldn't consider it a love story. <b>****Partial Spoilers****</b> Maybe a heartbreak story, but that's crossing the line. He talks a lot about his lost love and feels sad and stalks her and in the end, just realizes that <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Sometimes, true love is just having friends <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. *Gag*<br><br>The third story is Arianne's story, which I wasn't crazy about. Fourth was the valentine's story of Luce and Daniel. That's right, the ones the whole series are devoted to. I don't know why this was necessary; the entire FALLEN series is their perpetual and gag-worthy love story. This story I mostly skipped over.<br><br>At the end of the book is a snippet of the next (and last, thank God) book in the Fallen series, RAPTURE. I will admit I was really excited for this. FALLEN IN LOVE was a huge disappointment, and I thought I'd like the RAPTURE sneak-peek more.<br><br>I didn't.<br><br>It was boring, and I skipped over a lot of it. I hope the book reads more smoothly than the excerpt that was included, because if that's how the rest will be, I'm not so excited for it anymore.<br><br>FALLEN IN LOVE was a big disappointment in the world of FALLEN. Hopefully RAPTURE will redeem it a little bit.<br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br>Wow, cover model. Don't bend over, or your boobs will fall out of your shirt.<br><br><br><b>Edit: 1.15.12</b><br>OMG it's on NetGalley!<br>Request, request, request.<br><br>By the way, THEY NEED TO ACCEPT ME FOR ENDURE BECAUSE I NEED IT BEFORE I NEED FOOD.</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

  <b>
    <u>If you wish to read this novella on your own, without knowing anything about it... stop here.<br>Do not push the <i>View Spoiler</i> button. </u>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1467020197ra/19540380.gif" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br>1) The first starts with <u>Miles and Shelby</u>.<br>They just left Daniel back in time, where they saw Cam's heart beeing brocken and why he turned to dark side, but instead of just returning home to their normal time.... they find themselfs in yet another past.<br><br>In this one Lucindais already in love with Daniel but doesn't think that anything can happen between them because she is just a poor girl and he literally is a Knight in shining armor.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1495760600ra/22853855.gif" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>(side note: I just love Danny! He is the best.)</i><br><br>Aaaaaaaanyway.... What was I saying...?<br>Oh right!<br>They make a plan to help Lucinda get her Daniel and in the meantime fall in love with eachother.<br><i>(Kinda out of the blue if you ask me but whatever....)</i><br><br><br><br>2)Meanwhile <u>Roland</u> from their time has also landed on the same timeline as the other two and decide to help them with making sure Daniel will go to the Valentine festival that is going on.<br><br>However he get's sidetracked when he remembers that this is the place where five years ago he met his one true and only love.<br>He takes a trip down on memory lane and goes to her home and starts reminiscing about their past and the way he had to break her heart because he wouldn't be able to tell her the truth about his identity.<br><br>He then finds out that she's gotten married and is expecting her second child.<br><br>Heart aching, he runs into Ariane who just made sure that Daniel will be present at the festival.<br><br><br><br>3) <u>Ariane's love story.</u><br>Ok, truth be told this story and only this story, is worth reading the book.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1495760600ra/22853856.gif" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>A long time ago... Ariane was hiding on a dark cloud with Annabelle and Gabbe, when a beautiful Angel came into view. She said that her name was Tessriel, that she was their sister and told them that she had a message from Roland.<br>Gabbe got mad at her and sent her away telling her that Roland was with the Devil now and that they didn't want to hear any messages from Hell.<br>But Ariane was mesmerized by the Angel's beauty.<br>With a sad look towards Ariane, Tess flew away.<br><br>Years later while Ariane was walking alone by a lakeside, she saw the beautiful Angel again.<br>This time before she could say anything, Tess kissed her telling her that she promised herself that if they ever met again, she would kiss her.<br>Thus began their relationship.<br><br>Hundreds of years, since the fall... Ariane picked a side. She went back to the "Throne" and got her "white" Wings back.<br>Tess also had made a choice. She chose the Devil's side and her Wings turned to gold.<br>When each of them so the others Wings, they were shocked. Neither had told the other one of their plans of chosing.<br>The only thing they could do was break up.<br><br>More years later, Roland brought them back together and since that time they were into hiding from the other Angels since their love was forbidden.<br><br>When Tess had enough of hiding around, she pleaded Ariane to join her on the Devil's side so they could be together but Ariane refused.<br>In her heartbreak Tess mutilated herself with a starshot in hopes of killing herself.<br>Ariane found her bleeding and tried to stop her. They fought for the starshot and Ariane got some of Tesses blood on her. Mixed with her own blood, she got huge scars that will never heal.<br>When she realized that there wasn't anything that she could do, she flew away, promising Tess that she would send help.<br><br><i>(We don't really get to know what happened to Tess then but it is safe to assume that she died.)</i><br><br><br><br>4) Lastly we have another <u>Lucinda and Daniel</u>, past story.<br>They meet.... they kiss....<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1495760600ra/22853857.gif" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>you know the drill.<br><br> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_225497452" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/225497452" />
    <a title="Donna {Book Passion For Life}" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3024878-donna-book-passion-for-life"><img alt="Donna {Book Passion For Life}" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1563622982p2/3024878.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/225497452?book_show_action=true">Oct 19, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Donna {Book Passion For Life}" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Donna {Book Passion For Life}" href="/user/show/3024878-donna-book-passion-for-life">Donna {Book Passion For Life}</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9780385742610" href="/book/show/12629670-fallen-in-love">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024878-donna-book-passion-for-life?shelf=ya-paranormal-romance">ya-paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024878-donna-book-passion-for-life?shelf=for-review">for-review</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer225497452" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9087946055737806494"><i>Fallen in Love</i> is a novel which tells the tales of Miles, Shelby, Roland, Arriane, Luce and Daniel finding love on Valentine’s Day in Medieval England. With four different stories and each one completely different from the other, it was nice to see them all come together at the end to help Daniel and Luce have their perfect Valentine’s day. I did enjoy the single stories, some more than others but I don’t think it’s something you have to read in order to continue with the series. So read it or d</span>
  <span id="freeText9087946055737806494" style="display:none"><i>Fallen in Love</i> is a novel which tells the tales of Miles, Shelby, Roland, Arriane, Luce and Daniel finding love on Valentine’s Day in Medieval England. With four different stories and each one completely different from the other, it was nice to see them all come together at the end to help Daniel and Luce have their perfect Valentine’s day. I did enjoy the single stories, some more than others but I don’t think it’s something you have to read in order to continue with the series. So read it or don’t read it….it’s your choice but I’m glad I did and here are my thoughts.<br /><br /><b>Love Where You Least Expect It: The Valentine of Shelby and Miles.</b><br />I’ll be honest Shelby and Miles have never really been my favourite characters because I always felt they were quiet bland and were just put into the story to fill the pages. But after reading their story, I do feel more connected to them than before. Did I feel their story was necessary to the series? Not really. With or without it, it doesn’t make much of a difference but I guess it was nice to see them both falling love with each other. What I did enjoy was that they were as loyal to Luce as ever during this story and a girl always needs friends like them around.<br /><br /><b>Love Lessons: The Valentine of Roland.</b><br />Roland’s story actually surprised me. Talk about HEART-BREAKING! Poor Roland. He tries to come to terms with the fact that he's fallen in love with a mortal girl and knowing that they don’t have a future together. So, he does the only thing he can think of that will be for the best; he leaves but he does try to return a few years later only to see the girl happily married to someone else. The sacrifice Roland makes to keep this girl happy is unbelievable and it made me fall in love with him. What I really enjoyed about this story was getting that extra insight on Roland as a character because you don’t see that in the series and mainly how deeply he cares for Arriane whose friendship means more to him than anything.<br /><br /><b>Burning Love: The Valentine of Arriane.</b><br />I’ve always been a fan of Arriane, I really like her and her character is so unpredictable. Well, let me tell you this story definitely is unpredictable. Like all the others it’s Arriane’s love story but you would think it would be with a guy? WRONG! It’s with a girl named Tess and Lauren Kate definitely pulled out all the stops with this story. I think I enjoyed this story the most because it was fantastic to see Arriane in a different light but her story sure was heart-breaking. Falling in love with a girl that follows Lucifer is bad enough but when the girl asks you to changes sides for her is even worse. Good thing Arriane knows she belongs on the good side of the fight but it means her relationship with Tess is doomed and they don’t have future together. It’s a sad story but still good but I’d recommend you have a tissue ready.<br /><br /><b>Endless Love: The Valentine of Daniel and Lucinda.</b><br />This was the story I was looking forward to most of all because it’s more time with Daniel and Luce, but I didn’t enjoy it as much as I would of thought. Luce goes into Lucinda’s body so she can spend one Valentine’s Day with Daniel but she doesn’t really get to spend that much time with him. You read about her speaking with Bill, you read about her getting ready and all the while I was screaming for Daniel to come into the story. However, when he does it’s just like old times and it reminded me why I enjoy this series so much but it was just kind of the same old – the same information we’ve read previously about their relationships, except they do kind of get a happy ending on that one day. Overall it wasn’t really anything new and it’s not really necessary to the actual story but overall enjoyable. <br /><br /><b>Sneak peek into Rapture;</b> Yes, there’s a sneak peek into Rapture at the end of this book but I didn’t read it. I’m crazy, lol….I’m dying to know what happens next but I didn’t want to start the story and not be able to finish it off because I’d have to wait another 5 months……that’s torture. So I’m going to bare with it and wait until June.<br /><br /><i>Thank you to the publishers for providing me with a copy for review.</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="9087946055737806494" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_270339998" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/270339998" />
    <a title="Kirsten" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7468140-kirsten"><img alt="Kirsten" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1334461197p2/7468140.jpg" /></a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">People who like romance :)</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer270339998&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer270339998" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3911715719606929172">Read this... woooow <br/><br/>SPOILERS:<br/><br/>I gave this piece of shit "book" five stars because of Arrianes story. She should have just wrote a really long even more interesting version of that and called it Arrianes story and this would be awesome. <br/><br/>So all of you curious little love birds that like to read spoilers like me.. i give you a rap of each one.YAY REAL REVIEW TIME!<br/><br/>Love Where You Least Expect It: The Valentine of Shelby and Miles:<br/>this story blew my mind. no actually it made me want to blow up my mind </span>
  <span id="freeText3911715719606929172" style="display:none">Read this... woooow <br /><br />SPOILERS:<br /><br />I gave this piece of shit "book" five stars because of Arrianes story. She should have just wrote a really long even more interesting version of that and called it Arrianes story and this would be awesome. <br /><br />So all of you curious little love birds that like to read spoilers like me.. i give you a rap of each one.YAY REAL REVIEW TIME!<br /><br />Love Where You Least Expect It: The Valentine of Shelby and Miles:<br />this story blew my mind. no actually it made me want to blow up my mind it was so mindless and boring. So while sweet miles and bitchy Shelby are off looking for Luce they get lost in a little town where its almost valentines day and they fall in love. woo hoo. not. they have no sparks.. the love Kate forced on them is so unnatural.. i thought miles was all uber obsessed with Luce and now all of the sudden he and Shelby are doing it next to a medevil Calderon while Roland rides up on his white horse all golden dreadlocks and pissy. And whats with every single character being white, skinny, and american. sure we got one black guy and some half mutilated gargoyle devil... still<br /><br /> Love Lessons: The Valentine of Roland:<br />this story was okay.. apparently Roland loved some rich white girl in old times where black dudes are today's ghetto white trash. anyway they had planned to run away together (how sweet) but while she was miss rich white girl, she was also a HUMAN rich white girl. Roland says to cam he could change with her, but Rosaline (white girl) doesn't know about his demoness, so Roland does the noble (kiss my ass, nobleness) and breaks her poor rich girl heart by leaving her to live a normal demon free life. well Roland comes back from present day to get her back to find she moved on and has a family (hubby and kids) and just as poor white girl is going to loose her other lovely love (white version) to battle; Roland comes and makes it so white lover boy can stay with his family. how nice of Roland. (no offense intened with the whole "white girl" thang :))<br /><br />Burning Love: The Valentine of Arriane:<br />Awww this story was amazing. And here is what happened in my biased opinion of these tragic love stories for all of you who just want to read Arrianes story! so it all starts off with Arriane and Tess (yeas Arrianes long lost amazing love is a GIRL which makes it so much more beautiful in my opinion)hanging out in a meadow thing braiding hair and telling stories. Then they begin to fight [:'(] because you see, Tess is a demon, a very powerful demon who is very close to Lucifer. And as we all know sweet, but crazy little Arriane is not. They fight about the fact that Tess has to go back to the devils side and she wants Arriane to come with her. They start to physically fight and when Arriane leaves after saying goodbye, she senses something wrong and she goes to back to find that poor love struck Tess has tried to rip off her wings with (i think) a star shot (not sure). And apparently angel blood is like acid to another (not entirely sure if its for angel/ demon blood or just all angels in general) and Tess in bleeding, Arriane is bleeding from fighting with Tess and when Arriane trys to help Tess she gets burned.. that's how she got her scars. Since shes so weak she has to leave Tess and send someone to help. that's really the end. Its so tragic and sad and beautiful and I LOVED IT!!<br /><br /> Endless Love: The Valentine of Daniel and Lucinda<br />And finally.. this is practically just Luce and a old version of Daniel making out in a forest. that's all that really happens! WAIT.. she dances with Cam and he says some MYSTERIOUS things. wtf else is new. and this is supposedly the only valentine Daniel and Luce will share. <br /><br />And you get a sneak peak of RAPTURE. I really hope Kate will give us all the fucking answers finally.</span>
  <a data-text-id="3911715719606929172" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer4372021469244310764">Reading this for the second time made me realise just how much I had forgotten! It was so good to delve back into these little side stories to see the different kinds of love and relationships. There was heartbreak but there was also joy and comfort. We were able to learn a little more about a couple of characters plus see a new relationship blossom! Overall, if you have any interest in the Fallen series, definitely check this novella out! It is not essential to the overall plot but it does give</span>
  <span id="freeText4372021469244310764" style="display:none">Reading this for the second time made me realise just how much I had forgotten! It was so good to delve back into these little side stories to see the different kinds of love and relationships. There was heartbreak but there was also joy and comfort. We were able to learn a little more about a couple of characters plus see a new relationship blossom! Overall, if you have any interest in the Fallen series, definitely check this novella out! It is not essential to the overall plot but it does give more backstory to some really great characters.</span>

<div id="review_309253808" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/309253808" />
    <a title="Heather" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4825071-heather"><img alt="Heather" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1595786304p2/4825071.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/309253808?book_show_action=true">Apr 09, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Heather" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Heather" href="/user/show/4825071-heather">Heather</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4825071-heather?shelf=dresses">dresses</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4825071-heather?shelf=dark-romance">dark-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4825071-heather?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer309253808" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2373618465292862085">A-MA-ZING!<br/><br/>*Spoilers from now on!!*<br/><br/><br/>'Love where you least expect it' <br/>(The valentine of Miles and Shelby) :<br/><br/>This story follows Miles and Shelby as they step out of an announcer and into Medieval times, or more specifically, into the middle of a Valentine's faire!<br/><br/>I really enjoyed this as it gave more depth into the two's relationship and saw it develop more without any distractions/life-changing missions.<br/><br/>'Love Lessons'<br/>(The valentine of Roland)<br/><br/>This one was heart-felt and beautifully written as it also</span>
  <span id="freeText2373618465292862085" style="display:none">A-MA-ZING!<br /><br />*Spoilers from now on!!*<br /><br /><br />'Love where you least expect it' <br />(The valentine of Miles and Shelby) :<br /><br />This story follows Miles and Shelby as they step out of an announcer and into Medieval times, or more specifically, into the middle of a Valentine's faire!<br /><br />I really enjoyed this as it gave more depth into the two's relationship and saw it develop more without any distractions/life-changing missions.<br /><br />'Love Lessons'<br />(The valentine of Roland)<br /><br />This one was heart-felt and beautifully written as it also gave more depth into Roland. The story follows how he remembers the one mortal girl he ever loved, Rosaline. He too is also in the same time as the Medieval Valentine's fair and briefly bumps into Miles and Shelby. I personally LOVED how all the stories flowed into one another easily and without confusion.<br /><br />The valentine of Roland was one of the sad stories though and teaches him a lesson of losing love. It ends with him seeing Rosaline after 5 years but he does not show himself as she is happily married and with a child.<br /><br />He fights with her husband as he is a knight and her husband was leaving Rosaline to fight in the crusades. Roland wins the fight and tells him to go home and be with his family whilst he will take him place as a knight. It was such a sweet action and i admit, I almost cried.<br /><br />'Burning Love'<br />(The valentine of Arianne)<br /><br />Okay so this one was also quite sad and emotional and like I said before, it was nice to read from the charcter's perspective and give an insight as to how they act/feel.<br /><br />The story follows Arianne (also near the faire) and how her love, Tess, who sided with Lucifer and is a demon. The story follows how Tess wants her to join her and Lucifer so they can tell everyone about their love and won't have to hide anymore. Arianne, however, does not want to side with him and does not want to become someone else just for love.<br /><br />This story also almost made me cry as Arianne leaves Tess near the end but then returns when she gets a feeling Tess is in trouble, or injured. As it turns outl Tess, broken-hearted from loosing Arianne, had self-inflicted almost fatal injuries to her wings using a starshot (the only weapon that can kill/hurt an angel or demon) and is bleeding severely. Arriane tries to help her but Tess's blood touches hers accidently and burns Arriane's body badly, hence the name of the title.<br /><br />Definately one of the more rememberable stories.<br /><br />'Endless Love'<br />(The valentine of Daniel and Luce)<br /><br />Finally, we reach the valentine faire and we get to see Luce go '3D' into her past self (go into her body) for the faire. This Lucinda is heartbroken as Daniel, a knight, has not appeared at the faire. Luce, whilst looking for Daniel, bumps into Cam whilst dancing. Although this is the medieval Cam so she cannot share her problems with him.<br /><br />Eventunally, Daniel turns up and the two go off and share treasured time in the forrest together.<br /><br />My favourite part was the epilogue as the musicians who had been playing at the faire, lifted their masks at the end of the day and were revealed to be Roland, Arriane, Miles and Shelby! It was just a surprise to me and I thought it made a nice ending that they had been watching over Daniel and Luce.<br /><br />Overall, I loved <b> all <b> the stories!<br /><br />I recomend this as a quick read and any fan (like me) who is waiting VERY impatiently for the final 'Fallen' book to be released!!</b></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="2373618465292862085" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer2078642439096169379">This is just a few short stories about side characters in the <i>Fallen</i> series. Roland's story was great and gave him some much needed development, Shelby's was the same, though not quite as good, the other two are horrendously forgettable. If you're a fan of this series then read this one (before the final book). It's not needed but it's a good look at some other characters that don't get enough focus.</span>

<div id="review_272193798" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/272193798" />
    <a title="Amy Lignor" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6259268-amy-lignor"><img alt="Amy Lignor" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1442605454p2/6259268.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/272193798?book_show_action=true">Feb 04, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Amy Lignor" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Amy Lignor" href="/user/show/6259268-amy-lignor">Amy Lignor</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer272193798" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17745141741773648551">True Love Never Says Goodbye… Except for the reader, who reads these books with such intensity and passion that they almost want to strangle the publisher for having the nerve to offer an excerpt to the final Fallen book that they won’t be able to get their hands on for a few more months. <br/><br/>The Fallen series has become one of the largest and most well-known when it comes to the “winged ones” of the world, and Lauren Kate has managed to captivate and enchant all of her fans. Having this new novel t</span>
  <span id="freeText17745141741773648551" style="display:none">True Love Never Says Goodbye… Except for the reader, who reads these books with such intensity and passion that they almost want to strangle the publisher for having the nerve to offer an excerpt to the final Fallen book that they won’t be able to get their hands on for a few more months. <br /><br />The Fallen series has become one of the largest and most well-known when it comes to the “winged ones” of the world, and Lauren Kate has managed to captivate and enchant all of her fans. Having this new novel that offers four separate stories about our beloved favorite characters - just in time to make a very nice Valentine’s Day gift, by the way - is lovely. And the excerpt from Rapture - the fourth and final installment? Mouthwatering.<br /><br />As everyone knows who reads Ms. Kate, her characters have been through many lifetimes. There are present and past Daniel’s and Lucinda’s wandering the Earth in their own time periods, living out the inevitable moment where Luce will once again die the death of a passionate love that’s simply never going to be possible.<br /><br />The first story is all about one of my favorite duos - Shelby and Miles. Stepping out of their Announcer, they find themselves in medieval times where all Shelby wants to do is give Daniel and Luce just one day - one Valentine’s Day where they can be together, seeing as that for the rest of their lives it will never happen again. But what comes through is the sweetness and humor between the two characters as early signs of a relationship appear on the horizon. <br /><br />We then head into Roland’s word - the tough, the steel-spine, the man who is following Daniel in order to make sure the boy does NOT screw up in this lifetime. Roland’s not nearly as worried about Luce, seeing as that she seems to understand far more than the angel she’s in love with. This story, however, turns away from the path of the ‘Romeo &amp; Juliet’ couple, and offers fans a whole new look at the ‘Redemption of Roland.’<br /><br />Arriane and Tess, a relationship that tugs at the heartstrings, comes next. If not for a simple miscommunication, perhaps things could’ve been different. But a story where one will sacrifice for the other - no matter what the pain or agony is for punishment - is a true gift.<br /><br />And, of course, Daniel and Luce appear in story four to offer their fans a look at yet another ‘day in the life of.’ But this time, a day that meant beauty and joy on the one day devoted to love.<br /><br />Bad part of the book? The excerpt. No, before everyone goes getting all beside themselves in anger - I mean the fact that Rapture already sounds magnificent; a fulfilling ending to a stunning ‘out-of-the-box’ series…yet it’s not OUT YET! I know, I know, patience is a virtue. However, I’m more of a Cam, myself. Patience is one virtue I simply can’t get a handle on, no matter how many lives I live.<br /><br />Until Next Time, Everybody.<br />Amy<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="17745141741773648551" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">

                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1545610344" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7012916646657255581">I actually liked this book more than any book in the series I have read so far. Luce and Daniel's relationship is still getting on my nerves, but I absolutely loved reading about everyone else's relationship. It didn't matter if it was talking how the two people fell apart or how they grew together. I loved Miles and Shelby's relationship, and I loved watching it blossom. Miles finally got out of his funk, which was thinking that he was in love with Luce, even though he never had a shot when it </span>
  <span id="freeText7012916646657255581" style="display:none">I actually liked this book more than any book in the series I have read so far. Luce and Daniel's relationship is still getting on my nerves, but I absolutely loved reading about everyone else's relationship. It didn't matter if it was talking how the two people fell apart or how they grew together. I loved Miles and Shelby's relationship, and I loved watching it blossom. Miles finally got out of his funk, which was thinking that he was in love with Luce, even though he never had a shot when it came to the love between her and Daniel. </span>
  <a data-text-id="7012916646657255581" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_216113775" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/216113775" />
    <a title="Taneika" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5591031-taneika"><img alt="Taneika" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1564410672p2/5591031.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/216113775?book_show_action=true">Sep 27, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Taneika" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Taneika" href="/user/show/5591031-taneika">Taneika</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9780307976291" href="/book/show/12750561-fallen-in-love">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer216113775" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10948399818168892594"><b>More of my reviews can be found at <a href='http://flippingthroughthepages00.blogspot.com/ ' rel='nofollow noopener'>Flipping Through the Pages</a>!</b><br/><br/>*drools over cover*<br/><br/>I've done a mini review for each story :)<br/><br/><b>Love Where You Least Expect It: The Valentine of Shelby and Miles</b><br/>Rating: 1 star<br/><br/>Alrighty, first things first, I don't care about Shelby and Miles at all. Throughout the series so far, I think their both rather flat and boring. Miles sounds like every other guy with no personality and Shelby sounds like every other chick with no personality. <br/><br/>I don't think I have to explain thes</span>
  <span id="freeText10948399818168892594" style="display:none"><b>More of my reviews can be found at <a href="http://flippingthroughthepages00.blogspot.com/ " rel="nofollow noopener">Flipping Through the Pages</a>!</b><br /><br />*drools over cover*<br /><br />I've done a mini review for each story :)<br /><br /><b>Love Where You Least Expect It: The Valentine of Shelby and Miles</b><br />Rating: 1 star<br /><br />Alrighty, first things first, I don't care about Shelby and Miles at all. Throughout the series so far, I think their both rather flat and boring. Miles sounds like every other guy with no personality and Shelby sounds like every other chick with no personality. <br /><br />I don't think I have to explain these stories to you - they're pretty straightforward Valentine Day stories... I was hoping that this short story would make me care about Shelby and Miles more, but unfortunately it didn't. I felt like I was reading from Luce and Daniel's perspective again and so far, the two still haven't stood apart from any of the other characters. I felt it could've had the potential as it's stated that Miles is protective about his hat and Shleby wonders whether there is any sentimental meaning behind it - this doesn't get expanded on, and I feel it would have shaped Miles' character a lot more.<br /><br />As for the writing so far - it's still pretty satisfactory. <br /><i>"Lucinda hadn't even noticed - that was how lost in sadness she was"<br /><br />"One of his long golden-black dreadlocks came loose from its elastic and tumbled from the recesses of his helmet"</i><br /><br />That first example is a perfect case of telling rather than showing. There wasn't any need for the "lost in sadness" part, the reader gets it - she didn't notice something she should have, so she's clearly out of it, or sad (which had been mentioned multiple times beforehand). <br />As for the second example, I don't even understand that :|. I read that and had to do a double-take. If anyone can tell me how you have <i>golden-black</i> dreadlocks, feel free :)<br /><br />I must admit, one part did make me laugh - there is a cute part where Shelby goes to swap something and in order to get the item, she says that it's a mark of the devil and gets really theatrical about it. That made me laugh!!<br /><br />Overall, I was unimpressed, I didn't see a build in character or personality for either and would've liked to see that *something* that seperates them from the others in the Fallen series.<br /><br /><b>Love Lessons: The Valentine of Roland</b><br />Rating: 2 stars<br /><br />Okay, I guess I sort of felt for Roland more, and I definitely enjoyed his story more than Shelby and Miles'. I don't have a hell of a lot to say about Roland's story because whilst I was more interested in it than the former, the writing still wasn't that great and the story was only marginally better! <br /><br />HOWEVER, Roland's story helped clear up a plot hole-y type thing I picked up on in Passion. When Luce gives Daniel tattoos, why does he not have them in every other life? Turns out that angels can change their looks as they please and Daniel does it pretty much every lifetime (this may have been mentioned in Fallen or Torment but I can't remember), so yeah. I was happy about that.<br /><br />Then there's the cheesy love references...<br /><i>"At first, he was cautious in his ascent, but even in the creaky metal armor, he soon felt nimble again with light memories of love"</i> AWWWW.<br /><br />And we learn more about Cam, sort of. Kinda. Which was cool :)<br /><br />Yeah. That's about all I have to say about this one :|<br /><br /><b>Burning Love: The Valentine of Arriane</b><br />Rating: 4 stars<br /><br />NOW THIS ONE WAS COOL. <br /><br />Firstly Arriane's true love was a woman. A woman. I couldn't get over it. I initially thought that I read it wrong and they were just friends, but it seems I've underestimated Lauren Kate and she actually had the guts to write a gay character. I am so impressed! <br /><br />But you know what the saddest thing is? That I automatically assumed I read it wrong. We don't see enough gay characters in YA. Off the top of my head, I can think of Lola's parents (Dads) from Lola and the Boy Next Door, and now Arriane. And YA is my preference of genre! <br /><br />I thought Kate did Arriane's love story really well and I loved that this story had so much more happen than the others, there was actual drama, action and hurt. As the story develops, I was *this* close to shedding a tear for Arriane because I felt so sorry for her. <br /><br />As for the writing in this story, I thought it was definitely an improvement in comparison to the others (apart from the typos I found) and I was pleased to see another confirmation of how angel's bodies function. <br /><i>"Except for their wing scars, every other ink mark or wound or scar in time would fade away"</i><br /><br />Overall, I loved Arriane's story and I would have been extremely happy if this book just focused on her experiences.<br /><br /><b>Endless Love: The Valentine of Daniel and Lucinda</b><br />Rating: 2 stars<br /><br />This is 2 stars because I enjoy their story in general. But this was nothing new. It was the usual "I love Daniel", "If only Daniel were here..." "He had blonde hair (blah blah blah), but *insert long dramatic pause* he wasn't Daniel. *insert so called cliffhanger*.<br /><br />Yeah.<br /><br /><b>Overall</b><br />I loved learning Arriane's background and Roland's background (but mostly Arriane's!) and it was a nice, easy read. However, I really wish I actually cared about Shelby and Miles, and I'm really hoping to see more of them in Rapture. And the excerpt of Rapture was actually pretty interesting so I can say I'm somewhat looking forward to the last installment (AND GOD. I WANT TO KNOW WHY the curse has affected them, WHAT is so great about Luce? WHY does Lucifer wanna go all psycho and stuff-apart from the fact he is Lucifer and wants to destroy the world etc etc). <br /><br /><i>Whilst I received this from NetGalley, this has in no way affected my review</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="10948399818168892594" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_268483933" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/268483933" />
    <a title="Jennifer" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4317622-jennifer"><img alt="Jennifer" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1310704716p2/4317622.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/268483933?book_show_action=true">Jan 27, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer" href="/user/show/4317622-jennifer">Jennifer</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer268483933" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7277290804005246098">When Fallen debuted in December 2009, I fell in love with it. It was different than a lot of other YA novels out there at the time , which made it pretty refreshing to read. When Lauren Kate came out with the third installment in the Fallen series I was just as excited to read it as I was the other two, but my excitement quickly diminished-it seemed I was no longer interested in Luce and Daniel’s story anymore. I tried and could not finish the third in the series. With Fallen in Love, I thought </span>
  <span id="freeText7277290804005246098" style="display:none">When Fallen debuted in December 2009, I fell in love with it. It was different than a lot of other YA novels out there at the time , which made it pretty refreshing to read. When Lauren Kate came out with the third installment in the Fallen series I was just as excited to read it as I was the other two, but my excitement quickly diminished-it seemed I was no longer interested in Luce and Daniel’s story anymore. I tried and could not finish the third in the series. With Fallen in Love, I thought maybe I would have better luck.<br /><br />All of the short stories in Kate’s new novel are very sweet, there is no denying that. Kate takes you to a different time period and shows you the many types of love with each story, building up to the final Valentine story of Daniel and Lucinda. There is not much to say about each story individually as they are exactly what one can imagine. So, were they terrible to read? Not at all. Was I completely giddy reading them and so excited Kate published another novel? Not really. Publishing another novel revolving around other characters in the series is a good idea, but this one is so-so. The only perk is the sneak peak into her fourth installment, Rapture, which I happen to quite like so far.<br /><br />Why did I bother reading it? Because I want to like this series as a whole. It has elements to it that I adore and I want to recommend the series to those who share the same infatuations as I do (fallen angels-what’s not to love?) I look forward to reading the fourth and final book (out June 2012) just to see how it will all end.<br /><br />Overall: Debatable. Those who still love everything about the Fallen series will enjoy this compilation of short stories. They are sweet, they delve into the lives of other characters, and you get the sneak peak into Rapture. However, those that feel they may be in the same boat as myself will be left wanting more of the Lauren Kate that first started the Fallen series. So, here’s hoping the fourth book is a strong one…come on Lauren, you can do it!<br /><br /> Visit <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://endlessqueue.wordpress.com">http://endlessqueue.wordpress.com</a> for more reviews and bookish things!</span>
  <a data-text-id="7277290804005246098" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_241113120" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/241113120" />
    <a title="Tanja (Tanychy) St. Delphi/James" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4465641-tanja-tanychy-st-delphi-james"><img alt="Tanja (Tanychy) St. Delphi/James" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1330431599p2/4465641.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/241113120?book_show_action=true">Nov 29, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tanja (Tanychy) St. Delphi/James" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tanja (Tanychy) St. Delphi/James" href="/user/show/4465641-tanja-tanychy-st-delphi-james">Tanja (Tanychy) St. Delphi/James</a>
      </span>

          added it




        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer241113120" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6365131771564275427">I have no clue how to rate this half-books! Seriously this is published as a book, oh Dear Lord! I'll just say it surely isn't as good as first two (unfortunately) but it's a bit (but really little) better than third one (it's shorter thought)! <br/><br/>I wanted to jump out of my skin when I read "announcer", oh yes I still have nightmares after <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/9369720.Passion__Fallen___3_' title='Passion (Fallen, #3) by Lauren Kate' rel='nofollow noopener'>Passion</a>. Luckily it's only mentioned few times, so I survived. <br/>Basically here you have stories about Valentine's Day (now how sweet is that?). It's good because </span>
  <span id="freeText6365131771564275427" style="display:none">I have no clue how to rate this half-books! Seriously this is published as a book, oh Dear Lord! I'll just say it surely isn't as good as first two (unfortunately) but it's a bit (but really little) better than third one (it's shorter thought)! <br /><br />I wanted to jump out of my skin when I read "announcer", oh yes I still have nightmares after <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/9369720.Passion__Fallen___3_" title="Passion (Fallen, #3) by Lauren Kate" rel="nofollow noopener">Passion</a>. Luckily it's only mentioned few times, so I survived. <br />Basically here you have stories about Valentine's Day (now how sweet is that?). It's good because you find out something more about characters and also remember them. Yes that's problem with those books I don't have enough memory to remember who is related to who and everything, but that's my mistake. I got to say that the most interesting story was about Arriane (so you pay attention). <br />Maybe I sound too negative but really I'm not a heater and God knows how much I want to feel same joy that I felt within reading <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6487308.Fallen__Fallen___1_" title="Fallen (Fallen, #1) by Lauren Kate" rel="nofollow noopener">Fallen</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/7740152.Torment__Fallen___2_" title="Torment (Fallen, #2) by Lauren Kate" rel="nofollow noopener">Torment</a>, but the magic is not here. I don't know why and how it disappeared but I want it back badly. I still have hope that <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12716010.Rapture__Fallen___4_" title="Rapture (Fallen, #4) by Lauren Kate" rel="nofollow noopener">Rapture</a> will surprise me (please, please, please...). </span>
  <a data-text-id="6365131771564275427" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1436237484" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15590026626860474414">Ummm.... I actually don't know what to write? I don't understand why she even wrote this "book"?? Is it even long enough to class as a novel? no it isn't... Money money money *FACE PALM*<br/><br/>I have read the rest of the books and only have Unforgiven here left to read, is it just me that is glad to be at the end of this series? Don't get me wrong I liked Rapture it actually had a plot and I didn't want to rip my eyes from my head but I don't see why she had to try and slip Fallen in Love in there, pre</span>
  <span id="freeText15590026626860474414" style="display:none">Ummm.... I actually don't know what to write? I don't understand why she even wrote this "book"?? Is it even long enough to class as a novel? no it isn't... Money money money *FACE PALM*<br /><br />I have read the rest of the books and only have Unforgiven here left to read, is it just me that is glad to be at the end of this series? Don't get me wrong I liked Rapture it actually had a plot and I didn't want to rip my eyes from my head but I don't see why she had to try and slip Fallen in Love in there, pretty much a pointless book that you could go without reading.<br /><br />The book pretty much sums it up on the back cover, it is a story about the Valentine's day Luce &amp; Dan get to spend together. It also goes into how Miles &amp; Shelby first fell for each other and what went on with Roland &amp; Arriane's past loves which I found way more interesting and I wanted to read more! Then we get too spoiled Luce where everything revolves around her... damn you!<br /><br />Is the book a must read? No.. <br />Will you feel lost if you don't read it? No..<br />Worth the money? No..<br /><br />BUT if you are like myself and need to read every book in a series even if it's not the best I suggest you do because it's a lot better than the first 3 books, maybe Lauren was trying to redeem herself? <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="15590026626860474414" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground">Readers also enjoyed</h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent"><div class='bookCarousel'>
<div class='carouselRow' style='width: 3600px'>
<ul>
<li class='cover' id='bookCover_12751687'>
<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12751687-finale"><img alt="Finale (Hush, Hush, #4)" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/books/1362408156l/12751687._SX98_.jpg" />
</a>

  
<script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">
//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('3uk/xy15znjbmauQWZMxkZlvpHi5NWyIpcfF6veC6aimwBMO/lUPBEMKy0GWqA6255dT25TfLb52IB3nZJKa1w==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {

  }

Né come ci è arrivato, né perché. Indossa una divisa che non conosce, gialla come la luce che illumina la piccola stanza in cui è rinchiuso. Porta al polso destro un braccialetto senza fibbia simile a un display spento. Dove si trova? Non lo sa. I ricordi arriveranno poi, poco per volta. Scoprirà presto di non essere solo in questa misteriosa prigione. Con lui ci sono altri sei prigionieri. Ognuno ha ricevuto delle strane istruzioni da seguire, insieme a un curioso oggetto recapitato sotto la porta della cella. Hanno solo poche ore per salvarsi. Si parlano, si interrogano sul perché di quegli strani messaggi, cercano disperatamente informazioni e una via di fuga: litigano, si accusano vicendevolmente ma alla fine dovranno fare squadra… Perché c’è solo un modo per provare a uscire di lì. Fidarsi delle istruzioni. E degli altri… Anche se uno di loro forse mente.
